2,000 metres within just 20 minutes. The Nordkettenbahnen lifts welcome sightseers alongside sports fans with skis and snowboards. The lift stations are architectural highlights, designed as curved, glacial-like formations by star architect Zaha Hadid. The lifts provide a quick and easy way to access and experience the high alpine terrain above Innsbruck.</p><div style=\"text-align: right; font-weight: bold; font-size: 20px;\"><p><span that bears witness to centuries of history. A stroll through the city is filled with wonderful views of historical and natural highlights. The colourful buildings in the St. Nikolaus and Mariahilf districts are a famous example – behind them, the spectacular Nordkette mountain range soars up to 2,200 metres: a popular destination for recreation, relaxation and diverse alpine sports.</p><div style=\"text-align: right; font-weight: bold; font-size: 20px;\"><p><span style=\"color: #e2001a;\" class=\"glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right The Nordkettenbahnen lifts welcome sightseers alongside sports fans with skis and snowboards. The lift stations are architectural highlights, designed as curved, glacial-like formations by star architect Zaha Hadid. The lifts provide a quick and easy way to access and experience the high alpine terrain above Innsbruck.</p><div style=\"text-align: right; font-weight: bold; font-size: 20px;\"><p><span
